Act1: Forming the Alliance

Chapter 1

Library. Aged parchment s and musty to me s surrounded her, forming the very heartof knowledge that had
shaped the history of el doria. Asshe stepped further intothe hall,the morning light filtering in through the

from his reading."Ah, Seraphina.What brings you to the library so early?"
"I need your help with something," she responded,her tone weighted with curiosity and urgency."I
found a prophecy about ancient serpents."
A faint frown crease d Draco's forehead. "Ancient serpents?" he echoed, his tone laced with
skepticism. "Seraphina, legends of such creatures are ancient history. Do not waste your time on
unsubstantiated prophecies."
Seraphina sighed, frustration and doubt warring within her. she understood draco's skepticism,but
the words she had stumbled upon felt more than just some dusty legend. she pulled the ancient parchment
from her satchel, laying it gently on the table,the words inscribed on it a testament to the power of ancient
knowledge.
"I need to know if this prophecy holds any truth," she pressed, her eyes locking with Draco's. "I
can't ignore this."
Draco hesitate d before picking up the parchment, his fingers tracing over the text. Hiseyes scanned
the text quickly,then slowly. his expression shifted from doubt to intrigue,and then to worry.
"This is... disturbing," he murmured. "It talks about a time when ancient serpents will arise again,
unleash ing a wave of destruction. The last time such creatures were spoken of,it was before the fall of the
Elder Empire."
"Is there a chance it could be true,then?"Seraphina asked,her heart pounding.
Draco shook his head, uncertainty etched across his face. "It's just a prophecy, Seraphina. And
prophecies are...fickle things.they can be interpreted a hundred different ways."
"But what if it's not just another prophecy?" Seraphina pressed, her voice echoing through the

base our actions on what could be just a legend. But...," his voice trail ed off as he looked up at her, "I
understand your instincts. Keep looking, Seraphina. Keep investigating. Trust your instincts. Who knows

The room fell silent. Lily's gaze swept over the faces in the room, catching the fleeting glimpses of

Chapter 13
As the icy moon hovered over the treacherous landscape of frost v alle, detective lily harris on,her

within the foreboding woods.
Lily, her heart pounding relentlessly, felt the familiar chill in her veins, a familiarity she had grown
accustomed to since her first case involving the ancient legend. she knew that within those rickety wooden
walls, she would confront the leader ofthe cult—the one orchestra ting the Windigo's reign of terror.
The cabin door creaked open,revealing the dimly lit interior lit only by flickering candles.The cold
air outside gave way to a stifling warmth,almost as ifthe atmosphere was tinged with something sinister.
“This can't be good,” muttered Detective Lily harris on, her eyes scanning the room, a dance of
unease on her face.The scene inside was nothing short of nightmarish. There were grotesque idols and bones litter ing
the floor, and symbols drawn in blood de cora ting the walls. At the center of the room was a gruesome
sight—a makeshift altar upon which lay an unfortunate victim—the cult leader, donned in bloodied robes,
hovering over the body with anax.
"You've interrupted our ritual, Detective," the cult leader sneered at Lily, his voice raspy and
ominous. "Won't you pay for that dearly?"
But Lily was not one to be intimidate d. With an unwavering gaze, she retorted, "Your reign ends
here."
The leader let out a sinister chuckle as he brandish ed the ax, its blade reflecting the flickering
candlelight. "You're out numbered, Detective.You're no match for the power wehold."
With her gun aimed, Lily fired, catching the leader off-guard. He staggered back, blood seeping
through the robes,hisgaze now flickering with fear.
Her heart pounded harder as the cult members turned to face her. “Burn it,” she commanded,
motioning toward the windigo idol.
Officer Monroe and Dr. Blackwood nodded in unison, their grim determination mirror ing Lily's.
They grabbed whatever they could to set the horrifying idol ablaze—torches, burning rags, anything they
could use.
The wooden structure of theidol caught fire,its ancient symbols turning charcoal under the dancing

The flickering flames reflected in lily's eyes,a sense of triumph mixed with horror. her hands were
shaking slightly,but she pressed on.the battle was notwon yet.
Amidst the chaos, she made her way to the leader, the once menacing figure now crumpled onthe

She looked down at him, her eyes blazing with fury and determination. "This ends now," she

The echo of the gunshot rang throughout the cabin as the leader's body twitched and lay still. His

Chapter 14
As the last embers of the burning Windigo idol flicker ed and died, Detective Lily harris on took a
long, deep breath. Her heart pounded in her chest, the echo reverberating through the eerie silence that followed. The once-ominous atmosphere had now been replaced by an uneasy peace- a stillness that hung
heavily on the frigid air.
The aftermath of the horror unfolded around them, stark and devastating against the otherwise
picturesque backdrop of frost v alle. The usually quiet town had turned into a battlefield in the face of the
killing s thathad terrorize d its resident s.Yetnow,as thesun slowly peaked over the horizon,it shone alight
on the broken fragments of a community thathad survived the ordeal.
The local resident s, emerging cautiously from their homes, gathered around, their eyes wide and
faces etched with relief. It was as if they had awoken from a nightmare, relieved to find that it was over.
The authorities, led by the stern-faced Captain Thomas, were quick to move in, setting up a perimeter and
en sur ing that no further danger lurked in the snow-laden streets.
"We'll handle things here, Lily," Captain Thomas said, his voice echoing across the gathering

frost v alle captive for so long had finally been lifted.
Suddenly, a collective sigh echoed throughout the crowd, as if they were finally allowing

In the midst of the crowd, the familiar face ofDr.jonathan blackwood appeared. Hiseyes hadlost
